<script type="text/javascript">
function replaceAreaCidadaoButton() {
  const original = $('#area-cidadao-form input[type="submit"]');
  const cloned = original.clone();
  cloned.addClass('teste');
cloned.off('click');
  original.after(cloned);
  original.remove();

  cloned.off('click').on('click', function (event) {
    if ($('#area-cidadao-form input[name="agree"]').length == 0 || ($('#area-cidadao-form input[name="agree"]').length > 0 && $('#area-cidadao-form input[name="agree"]').is(":checked"))) {
$('#area-cidadao-form input[name="agree"]').prop('checked', false);
      event.preventDefault();
event.stopPropagation();
      event.target.disabled = true;
      const userName = getCookie('bdp_username');
      let queryObject = { t: Date.now() + "_" };
      if ($('#area-cidadao-form select[name="year"]').length > 0) {
        Object.assign(queryObject, { 'Ano': $('#area-cidadao-form select[name="year"]')?.val() });
      }
      if ($('#area-cidadao-form select[name="month"]').length > 0) {
        Object.assign(queryObject, { 'Mes': $('#area-cidadao-form select[name="month"]')?.val() });
      }
      if ($('#area-cidadao-form input[name="requires_auth"]')?.val() == '1' && userName === '') {
        Object.assign(queryObject, { 'return_url': $('#area-cidadao-form input[name="redirect"]')?.val() });
        let url = '/login/adfs';
        if (Object.keys(queryObject).length > 0) {
          if (url.includes('?')) {
            url += '&';
          } else {
            url += '?';
          }
          url += new URLSearchParams(queryObject).toString();
        }
        window.location.href = url;
      } else {
        let url = $('#area-cidadao-form input[name="redirect"]')?.val();
        if (Object.keys(queryObject).length > 0) {
          if (url.includes('?')) {
            url += '&';
          } else {
            url += '?';
          }
          url += new URLSearchParams(queryObject).toString();
        }
        $.ajax({
          type: "GET",
          url: url,
          crossDomain: true,
          cache: false,
          xhrFields: {
            responseType: 'blob'
          },
          success: function (data, textStatus, xhr) {
            if (xhr.getResponseHeader('content-type') == 'application/pdf') {
              const link = document.createElement('a');
              link.href = window.URL.createObjectURL(data);
              link.download = xhr.getResponseHeader('content-disposition').split('=')[1];
              link.click();
              event.target.disabled = false;
            } else {
              window.location.href = url;
            }
          },
          error: function () {
            window.location.href = url;
          }
        });
      }
    }
  });
}

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', replaceAreaCidadaoButton);
</script>

<div class="flexrow col-12">
<div class="flexone">
<h1 class="bdpsi-h1 title-container--title">Currency converter</h1>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="container">
<div class="prose">
<p>Calculations are made based on daily reference rates published by Banco de Portugal and the European Central Bank.<br/>When no exchange rate is available at weekends and on bank holidays, the exchange rate for the working day prior to the date requested is given.</p><p><strong>NB</strong>: The values are purely informational and not binding on the Banco de Portugal.</p><p class="bdpsi-primary clear-margins bdpsi-label-small-highcase"> </p>
</div>
</div>
